.mw-parser-output .hatnote{font-style:italic}.mw-parser-output div.hatnote{padding-left:1.6em;margin-bottom:0.5em}.mw-parser-output .hatnote i{font-style:normal}.mw-parser-output .hatnote+link+.hatnote{margin-top:-0.5em}@media print{body.ns-0 .mw-parser-output .hatnote{display:none!important}}

This article is about a list of countries and dependencies by population based on figures from official sources or, if not available, estimates and projections from the United Nations. For a list based purely on figures from the United Nations, see [List of countries and dependencies by population (United Nations)](/wiki/List_of_countries_and_dependencies_by_population_\(United_Nations\) "List of countries and dependencies by population (United Nations)").

This article reflects continually changing information from hundreds of sources. You can help by updating items to more recent figures from [official sources](#Method).

Population distribution by country in June-July 2025:

1.  [India](/wiki/Demographics_of_India "Demographics of India") (17.3%)
2.  [China](/wiki/Demographics_of_China "Demographics of China") (17.2%)
3.  [United States](/wiki/Demographics_of_the_United_States "Demographics of the United States") (4.20%)
4.  [Indonesia](/wiki/Demographics_of_Indonesia "Demographics of Indonesia") (3.50%)
5.  [Pakistan](/wiki/Demographics_of_Pakistan "Demographics of Pakistan") (2.90%)
6.  [Nigeria](/wiki/Demographics_of_Nigeria "Demographics of Nigeria") (2.70%)
7.  [Brazil](/wiki/Demographics_of_Brazil "Demographics of Brazil") (2.60%)
8.  [Bangladesh](/wiki/Demographics_of_Bangladesh "Demographics of Bangladesh") (2.10%)
9.  [Russia](/wiki/Demographics_of_Russia "Demographics of Russia") (1.80%)
10.  Others (45.7%)

This is a **list of countries and dependencies by population**. It includes [sovereign states](/wiki/Sovereign_state "Sovereign state"), inhabited [dependent territories](/wiki/Dependent_territory "Dependent territory") and, in some cases, constituent countries of sovereign states, with inclusion within the list being primarily based on the [ISO](/wiki/International_Organization_for_Standardization "International Organization for Standardization") standard [ISO 3166-1](/wiki/ISO_3166-1 "ISO 3166-1"). For instance, the [United Kingdom](/wiki/United_Kingdom "United Kingdom") is considered a single entity, while the constituent countries of the [Kingdom of the Netherlands](/wiki/Kingdom_of_the_Netherlands "Kingdom of the Netherlands") are considered separately. In addition, this list includes certain [states with limited recognition](/wiki/List_of_states_with_limited_recognition "List of states with limited recognition") not found in ISO 3166-1. Also given in a percentage is each country's population compared with the [world population](/wiki/World_population "World population"), which the [United Nations](/wiki/United_Nations "United Nations") estimated at 8.232 billion as of 2025.[\[1\]](#cite_note-UNFPA-1)

Method
------

See also: [List of countries and dependencies by population density](/wiki/List_of_countries_and_dependencies_by_population_density "List of countries and dependencies by population density") and [List of regional organizations by population](/wiki/List_of_regional_organizations_by_population "List of regional organizations by population")

Figures used in this chart are based on the most up-to-date estimates or [projections](/wiki/Population_projection "Population projection") by the national [census](/wiki/Census "Census") authority, where available, and are usually rounded off.

Where updated national data are not available, figures are based on the estimates or projections for 2024 by the Population Division of the [United Nations Department of Economic and Social Affairs](/wiki/United_Nations_Department_of_Economic_and_Social_Affairs "United Nations Department of Economic and Social Affairs").

Because the compiled figures are not collected at the same time in every country, or at the same level of accuracy, the resulting numerical comparisons may create misleading conclusions. Furthermore, the addition of figures from all countries may not equal the world total.

Areas that form integral parts of [sovereign states](/wiki/Sovereign_state "Sovereign state"), such as the [countries of the United Kingdom](/wiki/Countries_of_the_United_Kingdom "Countries of the United Kingdom"), are counted as part of the sovereign states concerned. Not included are other entities that are not sovereign states, such as the [European Union](/wiki/European_Union "European Union"),[\[a\]](#cite_note-2) and independent territories that do not have permanent populations, such as the [Chagos Archipelago](/wiki/Chagos_Archipelago "Chagos Archipelago") and [various countries' claims](/wiki/Territorial_claims_in_Antarctica "Territorial claims in Antarctica") to [Antarctica](/wiki/Antarctica "Antarctica").[\[2\]](#cite_note-3)

Sovereign states and dependencies by population
-----------------------------------------------

Note: A numbered rank is assigned to the 193 [member states of the United Nations](/wiki/Member_states_of_the_United_Nations "Member states of the United Nations"), plus the two [observer states to the United Nations General Assembly](/wiki/United_Nations_General_Assembly_observers#Current_non-member_observers "United Nations General Assembly observers"). Dependent territories and constituent countries that are parts of sovereign states are not assigned a numbered rank. In addition, [sovereign states with limited recognition](/wiki/List_of_states_with_limited_recognition "List of states with limited recognition") are also included, but not assigned a numbered rank.

Explanatory notes
-----------------

1.  **[^](#cite_ref-2)** The European Union is a _[sui generis](/wiki/Sui_generis "Sui generis")_ [supranational union](/wiki/Supranational_union "Supranational union") whose sovereign members delegate to it by treaty certain powers that are often exercised by sovereign states. Its combined population has been estimated at 447,319,916 on 1 January 2020, and it would be ranked 3rd if it were included in the list. It has 5.43% of the world's population — see .mw-parser-output cite.citation{font-style:inherit;word-wrap:break-word}.mw-parser-output .citation q{quotes:"\\"""\\"""'""'"}.mw-parser-output [European Commission](/wiki/European_Commission "European Commission").
2.  **[^](#cite_ref-6)** Includes the population of the [India-administered](/wiki/Kashmir_conflict "Kashmir conflict") [union territories](/wiki/Union_territory "Union territory") of [Jammu and Kashmir](/wiki/Jammu_and_Kashmir_\(union_territory\) "Jammu and Kashmir (union territory)"), and [Ladakh](/wiki/Ladakh "Ladakh").
3.  **[^](#cite_ref-8)** Referring to [Mainland China](/wiki/Mainland_China "Mainland China"); excluding China's [special administrative regions](/wiki/Special_administrative_regions_of_China "Special administrative regions of China") of [Hong Kong](/wiki/Hong_Kong "Hong Kong") and [Macau](/wiki/Macau "Macau"), which returned to Chinese sovereignty in 1997 and 1999, respectively.
4.  **[^](#cite_ref-10)** Includes the [50 states](/wiki/List_of_states_and_territories_of_the_United_States "List of states and territories of the United States") and the [District of Columbia](/wiki/Washington,_D.C. "Washington, D.C."), but excludes the [territories of the United States](/wiki/Territories_of_the_United_States "Territories of the United States").
5.  **[^](#cite_ref-13)** Excludes the population of [Pakistan-administered](/wiki/Kashmir_conflict "Kashmir conflict") regions of the [Kashmir](/wiki/Kashmir "Kashmir"); [Azad Kashmir](/wiki/Azad_Kashmir "Azad Kashmir") and [Gilgit-Baltistan](/wiki/Gilgit-Baltistan "Gilgit-Baltistan"), which, according to 2017 Pakistani census, had a population of 4,045,367 and 1,492,924 respectively.
6.  **[^](#cite_ref-18)** The [Bangladesh Bureau of Statistics](/wiki/Bangladesh_Bureau_of_Statistics "Bangladesh Bureau of Statistics") has a projection of 181 million for 2025, but this method derives from a base year of 2011. This same projection overcounted the population for 2022 by about 4.4 million.[\[12\]](#cite_note-17)
7.  **[^](#cite_ref-20)** Includes the [Republic of Crimea](/wiki/Republic_of_Crimea_\(Russia\) "Republic of Crimea (Russia)") and [Sevastopol](/wiki/Sevastopol "Sevastopol"), administrative areas on the [Crimean Peninsula](/wiki/Crimea "Crimea") occupied by Russia. The population does not include the [four annexed Ukrainian oblasts](/wiki/Russian_annexation_of_Donetsk,_Kherson,_Luhansk_and_Zaporizhzhia_oblasts "Russian annexation of Donetsk, Kherson, Luhansk and Zaporizhzhia oblasts"). The Ukrainian government and [most of the world's other states](/wiki/Political_status_of_Crimea "Political status of Crimea") consider the Crimean Peninsula, [Donetsk](/wiki/Donetsk_Oblast "Donetsk Oblast"), [Kherson](/wiki/Kherson_Oblast "Kherson Oblast"), [Luhansk](/wiki/Luhansk_Oblast "Luhansk Oblast"), and [Zaporizhzhia](/wiki/Zaporizhzhia_Oblast "Zaporizhzhia Oblast") parts of [Ukraine's territory](/wiki/Administrative_divisions_of_Ukraine "Administrative divisions of Ukraine").
8.  **[^](#cite_ref-32)** Excluding the three [British Crown Dependencies](/wiki/Crown_Dependencies "Crown Dependencies") and the 14 [British Overseas Territories](/wiki/British_Overseas_Territories "British Overseas Territories"), listed separately. Four British Overseas Territories are not listed due to a lack of permanent population. The four territories not listed are the _[British Antarctic Territory](/wiki/British_Antarctic_Territory "British Antarctic Territory")_ (an Antarctic territorial claim hosting only government officials and research station staff), the [British Indian Ocean Territory](/wiki/British_Indian_Ocean_Territory "British Indian Ocean Territory") (a military base), [South Georgia and the South Sandwich Islands](/wiki/South_Georgia_and_the_South_Sandwich_Islands "South Georgia and the South Sandwich Islands") (hosting only government officials and research station staff), and the [Sovereign Base Areas of Akrotiri and Dhekelia](/wiki/Akrotiri_and_Dhekelia "Akrotiri and Dhekelia") (a military base where permanent residency is limited to citizens of the [Republic of Cyprus](/wiki/Cyprus "Cyprus")).
9.  **[^](#cite_ref-34)** Including the integral 18 [regions of France](/wiki/Regions_of_France "Regions of France") (including five [overseas regions](/wiki/Overseas_departments_and_regions_of_France "Overseas departments and regions of France")). Excluding France's five [overseas collectivities](/wiki/Overseas_collectivity "Overseas collectivity"): [French Polynesia](/wiki/French_Polynesia "French Polynesia"), [Saint Barthélemy](/wiki/Saint_Barth%C3%A9lemy "Saint Barthélemy"), [Saint Martin](/wiki/Collectivity_of_Saint_Martin "Collectivity of Saint Martin"), [Saint Pierre and Miquelon](/wiki/Saint_Pierre_and_Miquelon "Saint Pierre and Miquelon"), and [Wallis and Futuna](/wiki/Wallis_and_Futuna "Wallis and Futuna"), and the [sui generis collectivity](/wiki/Overseas_France#Sui_generis_collectivity "Overseas France") of [New Caledonia](/wiki/New_Caledonia "New Caledonia"), which are shown separately. [Clipperton Island](/wiki/Clipperton_Island "Clipperton Island") (an uninhabited [state private property](/wiki/Overseas_France#Special_status "Overseas France") of France) and the _[French Southern and Antarctic Lands](/wiki/French_Southern_and_Antarctic_Lands "French Southern and Antarctic Lands")_ (including several [uninhabited islands](/wiki/Uninhabited_island "Uninhabited island") and an [Antarctic territorial claim](/wiki/Ad%C3%A9lie_Land "Adélie Land") hosting only government officials and research station staff) are not listed at all due to a lack of permanent population.
10.  **[^](#cite_ref-36)** Including [Zanzibar](/wiki/Zanzibar "Zanzibar").
11.  **[^](#cite_ref-45)** Does not include the [Rohingya people](/wiki/Rohingya_people "Rohingya people"). Some regions were estimated by satellite.[\[34\]](#cite_note-44)
12.  **[^](#cite_ref-60)** The last census was conducted in 1979. Sources disagree about the current population:
     
     *   The Afghani [National Statistics and Information Authority](/wiki/National_Statistics_and_Information_Authority "National Statistics and Information Authority") gives an estimate of 35,695,527 for 2024.[\[43\]](#cite_note-54)[\[44\]](#cite_note-55)
     *   The [Encyclopædia Britannica](/wiki/Encyclop%C3%A6dia_Britannica "Encyclopædia Britannica") gives an estimate of 36,432,000 for 2025.[\[45\]](#cite_note-56)
     *   The BBC gives a figure of 38.3 million for 2023.[\[46\]](#cite_note-57)
     *   The CIA gives an estimate of 40,121,552 for 2024.[\[47\]](#cite_note-58)
     *   The US Census Bureau provides an estimate of 49,552,566 for 2025.[\[48\]](#cite_note-59)
     
     All figures are mid-year.
13.  **[^](#cite_ref-66)** Includes the regions [Laâyoune-Sakia El Hamra](/wiki/La%C3%A2youne-Sakia_El_Hamra "Laâyoune-Sakia El Hamra") and [Dakhla-Oued Ed-Dahab](/wiki/Dakhla-Oued_Ed-Dahab "Dakhla-Oued Ed-Dahab"), the [disputed territory](/wiki/Regions_of_Morocco "Regions of Morocco") of [Western Sahara](/wiki/Western_Sahara "Western Sahara") administered by Morocco and excluding [Sahrawi Arab Democratic Republic](/wiki/Sahrawi_Arab_Democratic_Republic "Sahrawi Arab Democratic Republic") (see [Western Sahara conflict](/wiki/Western_Sahara_conflict "Western Sahara conflict")).
14.  **[^](#cite_ref-78)** Excludes the [Autonomous Republic of Crimea](/wiki/Autonomous_Republic_of_Crimea "Autonomous Republic of Crimea") and the city of [Sevastopol](/wiki/Sevastopol "Sevastopol"), Ukraine's _de jure_ territory which is occupied by Russia (however, includes the [Donbas](/wiki/Donbas "Donbas") region, [partly occupied by Russia](/wiki/2022_Russian_invasion_of_Ukraine "2022 Russian invasion of Ukraine")).
15.  **[^](#cite_ref-81)** Excludes the external territories of [Christmas Island](/wiki/Christmas_Island "Christmas Island"), the [Cocos (Keeling) Islands](/wiki/Cocos_\(Keeling\)_Islands "Cocos (Keeling) Islands"), and [Norfolk Island](/wiki/Norfolk_Island "Norfolk Island").
16.  **[^](#cite_ref-87)** [Taiwan](/wiki/Taiwan "Taiwan") includes [Penghu](/wiki/Penghu "Penghu"), [Kinmen](/wiki/Kinmen "Kinmen"), [Matsu](/wiki/Matsu_Islands "Matsu Islands") and other minor islands.
17.  **[^](#cite_ref-94)** Includes [Somaliland](/wiki/Somaliland "Somaliland").
18.  **[^](#cite_ref-99)** Excludes the three constituent countries of the [Kingdom of the Netherlands](/wiki/Kingdom_of_the_Netherlands "Kingdom of the Netherlands") in the Caribbean Sea ([Aruba](/wiki/Aruba "Aruba"), [Curaçao](/wiki/Cura%C3%A7ao "Curaçao"), and [Sint Maarten](/wiki/Sint_Maarten "Sint Maarten")), but includes the three special municipalities of the [Caribbean Netherlands](/wiki/Caribbean_Netherlands "Caribbean Netherlands") ([Bonaire](/wiki/Bonaire "Bonaire"), [Sint Eustatius](/wiki/Sint_Eustatius "Sint Eustatius") and [Saba](/wiki/Saba_\(island\) "Saba (island)")).
19.  **[^](#cite_ref-123)** Includes [East Jerusalem](/wiki/East_Jerusalem "East Jerusalem") and the [Golan Heights](/wiki/Golan_Heights "Golan Heights"). Also includes [Israeli settlers](/wiki/Israeli_settlement "Israeli settlement") within [Area C](/wiki/Area_C_\(West_Bank\) "Area C (West Bank)") of the [West Bank](/wiki/West_Bank "West Bank").
20.  **[^](#cite_ref-140)** Excludes [Kosovo](/wiki/Kosovo "Kosovo").
21.  **[^](#cite_ref-148)** Excludes the [Faroe Islands](/wiki/Faroe_Islands "Faroe Islands") and [Greenland](/wiki/Greenland "Greenland").
22.  **[^](#cite_ref-150)** Includes [Åland](/wiki/%C3%85land "Åland").
23.  **[^](#cite_ref-152)** Includes [Svalbard](/wiki/Svalbard "Svalbard").
24.  **[^](#cite_ref-155)** Excludes [East Jerusalem](/wiki/East_Jerusalem "East Jerusalem") or [Israeli settlements](/wiki/Israeli_settlement "Israeli settlement") in the [West Bank](/wiki/West_Bank "West Bank").
25.  **[^](#cite_ref-160)** Excludes the two self-governing associated states of the [Cook Islands](/wiki/Cook_Islands "Cook Islands") and [Niue](/wiki/Niue "Niue"), and the dependent territory of [Tokelau](/wiki/Tokelau "Tokelau").
26.  **[^](#cite_ref-168)** Excludes [Abkhazia](/wiki/Abkhazia "Abkhazia") (242,862, census 2011) and [South Ossetia](/wiki/South_Ossetia "South Ossetia") (53,559, census 2015).
27.  **[^](#cite_ref-Population_175-0)** Eritrea has never conducted an official government census.[\[143\]](#cite_note-PHS2010_full-169) Sources disagree about the current population:
     
     *   The UN gives an estimate of 3,502,000 for 2024.[\[144\]](#cite_note-UN_pop-170)
     *   The [Eritrea Ministry Of Information](/wiki/Cabinet_of_Ministers_of_Eritrea "Cabinet of Ministers of Eritrea") gives an estimate of 5.8 million for 2020.[\[145\]](#cite_note-171)
     *   The BBC gives an estimate of 6.2 million for 2023.[\[146\]](#cite_note-172)
     *   The [US Census Bureau](/wiki/US_Census_Bureau "US Census Bureau") gives an estimate of 6.4 million for 2025.[\[147\]](#cite_note-USCB_pop-173)
     *   [Encyclopedia Britannica](/wiki/Encyclopedia_Britannica "Encyclopedia Britannica") gives an estimate of 6,416,000 for 2025.[\[148\]](#cite_note-174)
     
     All figures are mid-year.
28.  **[^](#cite_ref-188)** Excludes [Transnistria](/wiki/Transnistria "Transnistria").
29.  **[^](#cite_ref-206)** Excludes [Northern Cyprus](/wiki/Northern_Cyprus "Northern Cyprus").
30.  **[^](#cite_ref-220)** _De facto_ independent, _de jure_ part of [Cyprus](/wiki/Cyprus "Cyprus").
31.  **[^](#cite_ref-226)** _De facto_ independent, _de jure_ part of [Moldova](/wiki/Moldova "Moldova").
32.  **[^](#cite_ref-232)** The political status of Abkhazia is disputed. Having unilaterally declared independence from [Georgia](/wiki/Georgia_\(country\) "Georgia (country)") in 1992, Abkhazia [is formally recognised as an independent state](/wiki/International_recognition_of_Abkhazia_and_South_Ossetia "International recognition of Abkhazia and South Ossetia") by 5 UN member states (two other states previously recognised it but then withdrew their recognition), while the remainder of the international community recognizes it as _[de jure](/wiki/De_jure "De jure")_ Georgian territory. Georgia continues to claim the area as its own territory, designating it as [Russian-occupied territory](/wiki/Occupied_territories_of_Georgia "Occupied territories of Georgia").
33.  **[^](#cite_ref-255)** [South Ossetia](/wiki/South_Ossetia "South Ossetia")'s status is disputed. It considers itself to be an independent state, but this is recognised by [only a few other countries](/wiki/International_recognition_of_Abkhazia_and_South_Ossetia#States_formally_recognising_Abkhazia_or_South_Ossetia_as_independent "International recognition of Abkhazia and South Ossetia"). The [Georgian](/wiki/Georgia_\(country\) "Georgia (country)") government and most of the world's other states consider South Ossetia _[de jure](/wiki/De_jure "De jure")_ a part of Georgia's territory.
34.  **[^](#cite_ref-284)** 882 residents regardless of citizenship, 618 citizens regardless of residence, 246 resident citizens.[\[250\]](#cite_note-va-283)
